GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::onResetStream(Http::StreamResetReason,\n   242→                                                                        absl::string_view) {\n   243→  const bool expected_reset = expect_reset_;\n   244→  const bool goaway = received_no_error_goaway_;\n   245→  resetState();\n   246→\n   247→  if (expected_reset) {\n   248→    // Stream reset 272→    Http::GoAwayErrorCode error_code) {\n   273→  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"connection going away health_flags={}\", *client_,\n   274→                 HostUtility::healthFlagsToString(*host_));\n   275→  // If we have an active health check probe and receive a GOAWAY indicating\n   276→  // graceful shutdown, allow the probe to complete before closing the connection.\n   277→  // The connection GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::onRpcComplete(\n   315→    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status, const std::string& grpc_message, bool end_stream) {\n   316→ handleFailure(envoy::data::core::v3::ACTIVE);\n   321→  }\n   322→\n   323→  // Read the value as we may call resetState() and clear it.\n   324→  const bool goaway = received_no_error_goaway_;\n   325→\n   326→  // |end_stream| will be false if we decided to stop healthcheck before HTTP stream has ended -\n   327→  // invalid gRPC payload, unexpected message stream or wrong content-type.\n   366→    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status, const std::string& grpc_message) {\n   367→  const char* service_status;\n   368→  if (!health_check_response_) {\n   369→    service_status = health_check_response_->status() != grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckResponse::SERVING) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid
